0                                   3233      30.              COPY  LISTPARM                List management defs
                                    3234             =*   A list header block is used to control access to a chain
                                    3235             =* of resources.  All elements which are to be linked together on
                                    3236             =* these doubly linked circular lists must have the elements
                                    3237             =* first word be space for a forward list pointer, and the second
                                    3238             =* word space for a backward list pointer.

                                    3247  1          =           LHEAD PFX=LH

                                    3372             =*********************************************************************
                                    3373             =*   Add elements to a list
                                    3374             =*
                                    3375             =*   Input
                                    3376             =*
                                    3377             =* &L  LADD     &HEAD,&FIRST,&FLAST,&FCOUNT,&WR=,&WR2=RAR,&WR3=EPAR
                                    3378             =*     &HEAD    is a pointer the head of the list (defop = LA)
                                    3379             =*     &FIRST   first element to be added to the list
                                    3380             =*     &FLAST   last element to be added (if not specified, assuming
                                    3381             =*              only one)
                                    3382             =*     &FCOUNT  count of elements being added (shouldn't be specified
                                    3383             =*              for only one add)
                                    3384             =*     &WR

                                    3386             =*     &WR3
